<script>
	jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
  const $target = $('.orange-call');
  if (!$target.length) return;
  const targetOffsetTop = $target.offset().top;
  $(window).on('scroll', function () {
    const scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
    if (scrollTop >= targetOffsetTop) {
      $target.addClass('stick-block');
    } else {
      $target.removeClass('stick-block');
    }
  });
});
</script>

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-href]').forEach(function(element) {
        element.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (!e.target.closest('a, button')) {
                window.open(this.getAttribute('data-href'));

        });
    });
});

<!-- Custom Tab headers to dropdown for post category filters 
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
  if (!$('body').hasClass('page-id-650')) return;
  
 $('.uael-post__header-filters-wrap').css('visibility', 'hidden');
  
  setTimeout(function() {
    function convertTaxonomyFilterToCustomDropdown() {
      const $filterContainer = $('.uael-post__header-filters-wrap');
      if (!$filterContainer.length) return;
      
      const $filterTabs = $filterContainer.find('.uael-post__header-filters li');
      if (!$filterTabs.length) return;
      
      const originalFilters = [];
      
      $filterTabs.each(function() {
        originalFilters.push({
          filter: $(this).data('filter'),
          element: $(this)
        });
      });
      
      const $dropdownContainer = $('<div>', {
        'class': 'taxonomy-dropdown-container'
      });
      
      const $customSelect = $('<div>', {
        'class': 'custom-select'
      });
      
      const $selectedDisplay = $('<div>', {
        'class': 'selected-option',
        'tabindex': '0',
        'role': 'button',
        'aria-haspopup': 'listbox'
      });
      
      const $optionsContainer = $('<div>', {
        'class': 'select-options',
        'role': 'listbox',
        'style': 'display: none'
      });
      
      $customSelect.append($selectedDisplay).append($optionsContainer);
      
      $filterTabs.each(function() {
        const $tab = $(this);
        const filterValue = $tab.data('filter');
        const optionText = $tab.text().trim();
        const isSelected = $tab.hasClass('uael-filter__current');
        
        // Create the option element
        const $option = $('<div>', {
          'class': 'select-option filter-option',
          'data-filter': filterValue,
          'role': 'option',
          'tabindex': '-1',
          'text': optionText
        });
        
        // Mark as selected if it's the current tab
        if (isSelected) {
          $selectedDisplay.text(optionText);
          $option.addClass('filter-option-selected');
        }
        
        // Add click handler for this option
        $option.on('click', function() {
          const selectedFilter = $(this).data('filter');
          
          // Update display
          $selectedDisplay.text($(this).text());
          
          // Hide options
          $optionsContainer.hide();
          $selectedDisplay.removeClass('open');
          
          $('.select-option').removeClass('filter-option-selected');
          $(this).addClass('filter-option-selected');

          for (let i = 0; i < originalFilters.length; i++) {
            if (originalFilters[i].filter === selectedFilter) {
              originalFilters[i].element.trigger('click');
              break;
            }
          }
        });
        
        $optionsContainer.append($option);
      });
      
      if (!$selectedDisplay.text()) {
        const $firstOption = $optionsContainer.find('.select-option').first();
        $selectedDisplay.text($firstOption.text());
        $firstOption.addClass('filter-option-selected');
      }
      
      $selectedDisplay.on('click keypress', function(e) {
        if (e.type === 'keypress' && e.which !== 13) return;
        
        e.stopPropagation();
        
        const isVisible = $optionsContainer.is(':visible');
        $optionsContainer.toggle(!isVisible);
        $(this).toggleClass('open', !isVisible);
      });
      
      $selectedDisplay.on('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.which === 40) { 
          e.preventDefault();
          $optionsContainer.show();
          $(this).addClass('open');
          $optionsContainer.find('.select-option:first').focus();
        }
      });
      
      $optionsContainer.on('keydown', '.select-option', function(e) {
        const $options = $optionsContainer.find('.select-option');
        const $current = $(this);
        const index = $options.index($current);
        
        if (e.which === 38) { // Up arrow
          e.preventDefault();
          if (index > 0) {
            $options.eq(index - 1).focus();
          } else {
            $selectedDisplay.focus();
          }
        } else if (e.which === 40) { 
          e.preventDefault();
          if (index < $options.length - 1) {
            $options.eq(index + 1).focus();
          }
        } else if (e.which === 13 || e.which === 32) { 
          e.preventDefault();
          $(this).click();
        } else if (e.which === 27) { 
          e.preventDefault();
          $optionsContainer.hide();
          $selectedDisplay.removeClass('open').focus();
        }
      });
      
      $(document).on('click', function() {
        $optionsContainer.hide();
        $selectedDisplay.removeClass('open');
      });
      
      $customSelect.on('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
      });
      $dropdownContainer.append($customSelect);
      $filterContainer.css('display', 'none');
      $filterContainer.before($dropdownContainer);

<script>  
//TOPBAR close button cookie 20250602
  jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    function setSessionCookie(name, value) {
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + "; path=/";
    }
    
    function getCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }
    
    if (getCookie('dogtv_banner_hidden_session') === 'true') {
        $('#topbar').hide();
    }
    
    $('.closetopbar .elementor-button').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        $('#topbar').slideUp(300);
        
        setSessionCookie('dogtv_banner_hidden_session', 'true');
    });
});
</script>

<!-- Expert Carousel - smooth swiper -->
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    setTimeout(function() {
        initInfiniteCarousels();
    }, 2000);
    function initInfiniteCarousels() {
        const carousels = [
            {
                selector: '.experts-carousel .swiper',
                speed: 80, 
                direction: 'left'
            },
            {
                selector: '.shows-carousel .swiper', 
                speed: 40,
                direction: 'left'
            },
            {
                selector: '.rev .swiper',
                speed: 40, 
                direction: 'right'
            }
        ];
        
        carousels.forEach(config => {
            const swiperEl = $(config.selector);
            if (swiperEl.length) {
                createInfiniteTicker(swiperEl, config);
            }
        });
    }
    
    function createInfiniteTicker(swiperElement, options) {
        const wrapper = swiperElement.find('.swiper-wrapper');
        const slides = swiperElement.find('.swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate)');
        
        const swiperInstance = swiperElement[0].swiper;
        if (swiperInstance) {
            swiperInstance.autoplay.stop();
            swiperInstance.allowTouchMove = false;
            swiperInstance.allowSlideNext = false;
            swiperInstance.allowSlidePrev = false;
        }
        
        if (wrapper.find('.swiper-slide-duplicate').length === 0) {
            const clonedSlides = slides.clone().addClass('swiper-slide-duplicate');
            wrapper.append(clonedSlides);
        }
        
        let isAnimating = true;
        let currentPosition = 0;
        let lastTimestamp = 0;
        
        const slideWidth = slides.first().outerWidth(true);
        const totalSlides = slides.length;
        const totalWidth = slideWidth * totalSlides;
        
        function animate(timestamp) {
            if (!isAnimating) {
                lastTimestamp = timestamp;
                requestAnimationFrame(animate);
                return;
            }
            
            const deltaTime = timestamp - lastTimestamp;
            lastTimestamp = timestamp;
            
            const pixelsToMove = (options.speed * deltaTime) / 1000;
            
            if (options.direction === 'left') {
                currentPosition -= pixelsToMove;
                if (currentPosition <= -totalWidth) {
                    currentPosition = 0;
                }
            } else {
                currentPosition += pixelsToMove;
                if (currentPosition >= totalWidth) {
                    currentPosition = 0;
                }
            }
            wrapper.css('transform', `translate3d(${currentPosition}px, 0, 0)`);
            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }
        
        requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        return {
            pause: () => isAnimating = false,
            play: () => isAnimating = true,
            setSpeed: (newSpeed) => options.speed = newSpeed
        };
    }
});
  </script>

<!-- Enhanced script to preserve URL parameters for both internal and external links -->
<script>
(function() {
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const paramsString = urlParams.toString();
    
    if (paramsString) {
        // Handle internal links (same domain)
        const internalLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="/"], a[href^="' + window.location.origin + '"]');
        
        internalLinks.forEach(function(link) {
            const href = link.getAttribute('href');
            const url = new URL(href, window.location.origin);
            
            urlParams.forEach(function(value, key) {
                if (!url.searchParams.has(key)) {
                    url.searchParams.set(key, value);
                }
            });
            
            link.setAttribute('href', url.pathname + url.search);
        });
        
        const externalDomains = [
            'watch.dogtv.com',
            'checkout.dogtv.com',
        ];
        
        externalDomains.forEach(function(domain) {
            const externalLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="' + domain + '"]');
            
            externalLinks.forEach(function(link) {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                
                try {
                    const url = new URL(href);
                    if (url.hostname === domain) {
                        urlParams.forEach(function(value, key) {
                            if (!url.searchParams.has(key)) {
                                url.searchParams.set(key, value);
                            }
                        });
                        
                        link.setAttribute('href', url.toString());
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    if (href.startsWith('/') && window.location.hostname !== domain) {
                        const newUrl = 'https://' + domain + href + '?' + paramsString;
                        link.setAttribute('href', newUrl);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();
</script>

					// Global page view and session tracking for UAEL Modal Popup feature
					try {
						// Session tracking: increment if this is a new session
						
						// Check if any popup on this page uses current page tracking
						var hasCurrentPageTracking = false;
						var currentPagePopups = [];
						// Check all modal popups on this page for current page tracking
						if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
							jQuery('.uael-modal-parent-wrapper').each(function() {
								var scope = jQuery(this).data('page-views-scope');
								var enabled = jQuery(this).data('page-views-enabled');
								var popupId = jQuery(this).attr('id').replace('-overlay', '');	
								if (enabled === 'yes' && scope === 'current') {
									hasCurrentPageTracking = true;
									currentPagePopups.push(popupId);
								}
							});
						}
						// Global tracking: ALWAYS increment if ANY popup on the site uses global tracking
												// Current page tracking: increment per-page counters
						if (hasCurrentPageTracking && currentPagePopups.length > 0) {
							var currentUrl = window.location.href;
							var urlKey = 'uael_page_views_' + btoa(currentUrl).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '').substring(0, 50);
							var currentPageViews = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(urlKey) || '0');
							currentPageViews++;
							localStorage.setItem(urlKey, currentPageViews.toString());
							// Store URL mapping for each popup
							for (var i = 0; i < currentPagePopups.length; i++) {
								var popupUrlKey = 'uael_popup_' + currentPagePopups[i] + '_url_key';
								localStorage.setItem(popupUrlKey, urlKey);
							}
						}
					} catch (e) {
						// Silently fail if localStorage is not available
					}
				})();

								jQuery.cachedScript = function(url, options) {
									options = jQuery.extend(options || {}, {
										dataType: "script",
										cache: true,
										url: url
									});
									return jQuery.ajax(options); // Return the jqXHR object so we can chain callbacks
								};

								let uael_particle_loaded = false; //flag to prevent multiple script loads.

								jQuery( document ).on( "ready elementor/popup/show", () => {
										loadParticleScript();
								});

								jQuery( window ).one( "elementor/frontend/init", () => {
								 	if (!uael_particle_loaded) {
										loadParticleScript();
									}
								});
								
								function loadParticleScript(){
								 	// Use jQuery to check for the presence of the element
									if (jQuery(".uael-particle-yes").length < 1) {
										return;
									}
									
									uael_particle_loaded = true;
									var uael_url = uael_particles_script.uael_particles_url;
									// Call the cachedScript function
									jQuery.cachedScript(uael_url);
								}
//# sourceURL=elementor-frontend-js-after
</script>
